<date>1522333400027</date>< rate>

< Review>
This is one of my go-to spots in the neighborhood. The food is up there with the tastiest Mexican food you can get with a great modern/neighborhood atmosphere. I love the outside dining area...even though it's on the corner of a somewhat busy intersection and you're looking at traffic, it's so nice to be able to take your food outside and enjoy it there.
The staff are super friendly and nice...and the place has always been really clean every time I walked in.
I've had the burrito, nachos, and a various tacos and my experience has been that if its on the menu its going to be good eats. You cannot make a bad choice here...everything tastes super fresh and great.
Word to the wise: if you are sensative to salsas, the mild is still SOMEWHAT SPICY...however it is SUPER tasty. The "hot" actually means hot. Proceed to flavortown with caution. ;-)</Review>

<username>sam oksner</username><response>None<//response><userid>103996560023307425396< /userid><Pics>None<//Pics>< Review>
Not a fan of their Salsa bar, very bland Salsa, and the Hot was barely spicy.

Seems like most food is assembled very sloppily. Burritos are uneven with guac on 1 side and just beans and rice in another corner.

Their hardshells tacos are different and very good IF you get them to put the guac and cheese INSIDE the shell, otherwise they lay the taco on its side and just throw it on top, making a mess, soggy shell and half the cheese in your plate instead of in the taco.

The steak tastes great and when they get the hardshells correct, 5 stars but they only get it right half the time so beware.<//Review>
